1Six years.

(October 1917 - October 1922 1)

Five years of tireless struggle. Five years of breaking the foundations of the old world. Five

years of uncontrollable rush towards the future. Five years of great shift. Old |
economic capitalist way of life, old sour way of life, old foundations |

family, morality, law, science, everything was shaken up, revealed with gaping sores
the rottenness of the old world. The clumsy, petrified brain of the Russian ordinary
The body is not yet able to grasp the grandiose process of the world revolution.

Not only ‘within the colossal spaces of Russia, not only in its
life, but in the life of the whole world there is a fierce struggle between red and black,
active with passive, dying with living.

there is no end to this great historical hurricane and there will be no end until then

until humanity comes to that social order, to that world where labor |.

will turn from a curse into. blessing, where is the genius of the brave and the labor of the free
will forge a new life. Great happiness to be a contemporary of this history.
ric period.

7Kiznь declared loudly: only the strong have a place on earth, only those who see
The horizons of the future are clear, only for those who carry everything on the battlefield - victory. This
does not fit into the understanding of the average person, timid, craving peace, pies and
jam, a serene life.

He is great, this common man. His rotten thought permeates every pore of life
and infects the new being born everywhere where the refreshing hurricane does not penetrate
revolution. `

To him, the common man, his poets and his scientists now sing hymns. For its wide
an old thought, knocked out of position, is hiding behind him, strength is trying to lean on him
of the old world: a merchant and a banker, a manufacturer and a priest, a headless intellectual,
lawyer, actor, doctor, former y All of them, both abroad and within the country
cultivate their furious hatred of the builders of the new.

Their eyes see only our mistakes; for them there is nothing in the great revolution.
On one positive side, they are only akin to that which at least slightly resembles
old and therefore NEP; this is their element, their hope, partial fulfillment of their
aspirations and hopes. g

For us, NEP is a tactic, a form of struggle between the old and the new. We know well
that there are comrades Marxists, communists, deafened by NEP, who did not understand
the meaning of the form, the nature of our struggle at this time. moment.

But the creative power of communism, the sharp political thought of the revolutionary
Marxism clearly reveals for us. all the complexity of the modern situation
New paths we need leading to the goal set for ourselves by communism.

1*
&

-4 -\

ъ “%

On the 5th anniversary of October we enter under the sign of struggle on the ideological
front. The struggle for the personnel of the leaders of the revolutionary economy,
politics, science, art, organization of all diverse branches of society
of life.

In a plant, factory, higher, lower and secondary school, in the field, in the forest, in
waters, confined in concrete straitjackets, in power plants, everywhere
a new young woman must grow up, or rather must be nurtured, raised by us,
a powerful outgrowth of communist creative forces. Strength from the masses, from the bottom,
out of 150 million peoplebottom layer, still saturated with the remnants of the bourgeois era
new dominion. And the 5th year of the revolution tells us:

'Be vigilant on the military front!
’ Be persistent, efficient, and confident on the economic front!

Be vigilant, persistent, confident, never stop creating, updating
on the ideological front!

We are entering a bloodless period, but cruel, merciless for life,
but to the death of the struggle between the two ideologies of communism and bourgeois ideology.

''It is infinitely complex, this struggle, diverse in its manifestations
from the smallest aspects of everyday life to the highest scientific and philosophical generalizations.

It is difficult on a daily basis and takes a long time to develop.

But the proletariat did not and does not have easy tasks.

And celebrating our entry into the 6th year of the revolution, we say:

The tasks are great, but our strength is powerful. The path is difficult, but didn't we know how?
bear on your shoulders 5 immeasurably difficult years of revolution.

The red banner still flies proudly above our heads.

And it still calls us without self-delusion, with full consciousness of thee.
I will challenge those standing before us with inexhaustible readiness for tireless
creative work - struggle. <

Forward to our great future!

A song about boredom.

Do you want an ax in the back?

To the autumn yard. | ]

Rough, sweaty, like labor;

New Physical Culture of the Proletariat.

1. The class nature of physical education.

Physical culture, like cultural
tour intellectual, emotional and
production (science, art and
technology) has always had the stamp of class
origin.

Proletarian sport and proletarian
gymnastics, according to its purely class
forms and tasks, differ sharply from
old physical culture of the bourgeoisie. Although
outwardly old sport and old gymnastics
seemed classless and universally human

technical, but in fact all are old

systems of sports and gymnastics were
through are impregnated with bourgeois ideology
gee.

The national German gym system
nastika “Tigpep” (i.e. resourcefulness)
Yana and all the success of gymnast societies -
tourners with a sharply political overtones
was just one form of aggressive
processions of German small trade bourgeois
juisie with its ideology of nationalism and
chauvinism after the Napoleonic wars.

Czech Sokol anthem system-
Tyrsha's sticks with her ideology of pansla-
dynasty and with all its “falcon rallies”
was only a method of revolutionary pro-
propaganda and nationalist organizations
morally minded oppressed Czech
bourgeoisie under the guise of cultural education
zealous and spiritual-moral efficiency
falcon bots (by the way, remember
Urapatriotism of the Sokol squads in
time of war and their White Guard action during
suppression of revolutionary outbreaks).

Dalcroze's aesthetic system
gymnastics with her view of beauty
movements in the form of relaxed fluid movements
of which gestures there is only a direct trace

/

the impact of the ideology of aestheticism, modernism
and decadence of large commercial and financial
financial bourgeoisie of the capitals of Europe.
Understanding of the dying, purely noble-
heavenly beauty of sleek movements,
refined, aesthetic rhythmic
Plastic surgery according to the Dalcroze system is available

even definitely of class descent

Rejuvenation.

_

Bringing back lost youth is
the eternal dream of humanity. Not a little
there have been attempts to find a means of "eternal
youth." In ancient times, people came
for this we went to various witchcrafts
and sacraments, and in the Middle Ages scientists
alchemists were diligently preparing
the influence of the “elixir of life”, which gives
supposedly eternal youth. But all of this was
only baseless fantasies.

At the end of the 19th century, the
scientific study of this subject -

t research into the causes of sta-

growth and the possibility of avoiding it
severe consequences. And here on the per-
in terms of the names of two scientists,
one Frenchman - Brown-Séquard, another

gogo Russian - Mechnikov; both work
thali in Paris.

Brown-Séquard in the 1980s
centuries made his famous experiments
you with “testicular emulsion”, i.e.
with an extract from the male gonads -
rabbit Having injected myself with this extract,
he suddenly felt an influx of strength and
youth. (He) was already at that time
an old man over 70). Tried on other
for some old people, this remedy is also in many
In many cases it had a rejuvenating effect
action. A new wonderful remedy can-
lodost caused delight and pain everywhere
high hopes. But soon it came
disappointment, ‘for it turned out that
eraun-Sekarovsky remedy’ action-

This is completely meaningless. Disappointing

Fine art studio of the Petrograd Proletkult.

{From April 1 to May 1 in a small room-
reading room at the Central Arena AllRussian-
of the Russian Proletkult (Hermitage) was opened
exhibition of works by Petrogradsky's IZO studio
Proletkult.

The opening of the exhibition was not advertised and
the circle of her visitors was extremely small.
Meanwhile, what the Petrograd Studio gave,
was of significant interest not only
in relation to identifying individual talents,
but also as an indicator of the clarity of the Studio’s work
in its entirety. Thus, all that remains is
regret that the exhibition was too closed-
ted character and was not used as
she deserved it.

What first of all drew attention to itself
mania in the works of Petrograders, this is the clarity of
tasks set in each individual case and
sustainability in their resolution. It's not always possible
but, of course, talking about attentiveness has achieved
changes, but if the reporting cycles of studio diseases

be considered as a material "not only for-
a certain period, but also pre-
defining the starting point for further
movement, then one cannot but agree with the fact that
and deviations from the intended path, if they
can be clearly taken into account, acquire substantive
the most important significance. In the works of Petrograd-
skaya Studio clarity of tasks as
times and entails convincing clarity
positive and negative decisions.
Hence the regret we have already expressed about
non-use of the exhibition, this is its pure
pedagogical significance

The tasks put forward by Petrograd residents can
be reduced to several main groups.
First subjected to comprehensive study
the entire surface of the painting, as containing
themselves one or another linear, planar,
volumetric and color-light relationships. By-
structure in a circle, semicircle, square, three-

Golnik—these are the titles of the works of this group.

such things, Buck for example, "Building in
square" by I. Larionov (silhouettes by the fire),
the problem is solved masterfully;

Thinning the atmosphere over the fire, the artist
divides plans along two curves giving
reverse repetition of the main lines of movement
silhouettes. Thus, the composition is entirely
fits into a square shape. In composition
to halfway houseruge “Array to the right, attention to-
left" the same artist puts forward the task
balance the purely picturesque moment of the moment-

volume of associative nature. Feeling mas
siva, establishing the center in the right segment
semicircle, opposed aspiration
the observing figure in the left sector. Createthea
the second center, and thanks to this, balance
in Vassa in the same plan G. Corno-
Ukhova (“Attention—explosion”) gives a different resolution
solving the problem. The basis is similar to the closing one
semicircle curve, and the movement unfolds
from left to right, fading into the right corner.

To the second group we include works on
"texture" tasks. Surface of the painting
organized in the splendor of what is applied to it
material, its dullness, roughness, ‘pain’
neck or less dryness, single layer and
multi-layer gaskets, etc.

Work that solves these problems has not come
tries to read the best of what Pete gave
Rograd Studio. There is no sufficient invention
efficiency in the application and processing of mathematics
rials, so whole pieces cannot be classified
to quote otherwise than “empty”.

The work of Yu. Bodnek is more serious than others, luckily
who used the solid fill technique
(black enamel) and powder (colorful poro-
shock and rusty tin).

But; Taking into account the experience of the past, we come to
to young writers with a different method
on their development.

The proletarian writer must be
connected with the masses every day, living their lives
completely. His upbringing as an artist
must go from here, Therefore its development
should not begin from studying theoretical
heavenly depths of poetry and prose, from life
practices.

LITO local work plan for this issue
research is being developed by us now that work
is carried out in three directions:

a) Correspondence to newspapers and magazines.

6) Creation and publication of your own newspapers and magazines
cash, starting with oral and wall newspapers,
cozy magazine, etc.

c) Collaboration with the local theo-studio
Proletkult or club, script processing
everyday scenes, ditties, fables, plays.

d) Development of poster texts, slogans,
texts for illustrations, etc.:

Working in the studio begins with studying
newspapers and forms of newspaper material.

Article, information, note, report, inter-
view, household news, newspaper technology
(excursions to the printing house), journalism of all
types, practical work, editorial,
program article, propaganda article, re-
license and above designated forms of newspaper
work.

And further, after passing through two half-
years of this cycle, work is already underway on the
literature in the generally accepted sense of the word.

This production sharpens the powers of observation.
young writer to his surroundings, closer
in the greatest possible way connects it with the life of the masses,
broadens his horizons through wide coverage
newspaper of world events; studying it in all
its elements, the proletarian writer emerges
far beyond the scope of armchair “political” art
good work. All this informs him
further creativity the greatest vital
ity and breadth of creative scope. Byuschzya
key on the pages of the newspaper political
life on a global scale, cancels the shadow
tendency to retreat into the shell of a formal relationship
passion for art.
